like all medicines , this medicine can cause side effects , although not everybody gets them . some of these effects may be serious and may require medical attention . as with similar medicines , rare cases of allergic reactions have been reported during general use of bondronat . it is important that you always contact your doctor immediately if you experience any of the following symptoms : - swelling of face , tongue or throat - difficulty breathing - abdominal difficulty or swallowing - sudden decrease or loss of vision - a skin rash which may be a sign of a serious allergic reaction . - if you notice any of these symptoms , please seek medical advice immediately . these may be signs of a serious allergic reaction . - if you notice any of the following , you must stop the injection and tell your doctor straight away . your doctor may decide to keep you under closer observation or change your medicine . stop using fluid-filled_sac_in_the_kidney and see a doctor straight away if you notice any of the following serious side effects : - you may need urgent medical treatment : - if you have a combination of any of the following symptoms : - swelling of face , tongue or throat - difficulty breathing - abdominal difficulty or swallowing - sudden decrease or loss of vision - a general feeling of heat in your body - these may be signs of a sudden drop in blood pressure . this requires urgent medical medical medical care . your doctor may decide to keep you under closer observation or change your medicine . stop using bondronat and see a doctor straight away if you notice any of the following serious side effects : - you may need urgent medical treatment : - if you have a combination of any of the following symptoms : - swelling of face , tongue or throat - difficulty breathing - abdominal difficulty or swallowing - sudden decrease or loss of vision - a general feeling of heat in your body - these may be signs of a sudden drop in blood pressure . this requires urgent medical medical medical care . your doctor may decide to keep you under closer observation or change your medicine . your doctor will monitor your child ' s medicines before and during the infusion and for at least six hours after the start of other infusions . if you have any further questions , please ask your doctor or your pharmacist . - this medicine has been prescribed for you . do not pass it on to others . it may harm them , even if their symptoms are the same as yours . - if you have any further questions on the use of this medicine , ask your doctor or pharmacist . in this leaflet : 1 . what xigris is and what it is used for 2 . before you are given xigris 3 . how xigris is used 4 . possible side effects

like all medicines , this medicine can cause side effects , although not everybody gets them . tell your doctor immediately if you develop any of the following serious side effects : severe and persistent pain in the abdomen ( stomach area ) which might reach through to your lungs with or without inflammation ( non - melanoma inflammatory syndrome ). if you develop symptoms such as swelling of the face , lips , mouth , tongue and / or throat , which may be signs of a serious allergic reaction . symptoms of swelling , pain and redness of the joints , which may be a sign of inflammation in the lungs ( osteonecrosis ). tell your doctor immediately if you develop symptoms of an infection ( for example , pain , and redness in the leg ), which may travel through blood vessels to the lungs causing chest pain and other frequent infections . if you have symptoms of swelling , pain and redness in your thigh , hip or groin as this may be a sign of an inflamed pancreas ( a common side effect that may affect up to 1 in 10 people ), but are extremely serious and patients should stop taking the medicine and see their doctor immediately . if these effects are not treated they could be fatal . serious side effects : if you notice a skin rash or ulcers in your mouth , please tell your doctor or nurse immediately . see a doctor immediately if you get symptoms such as swelling , pain , and redness in the leg or leg . these may be signs of bone damage in the jaw ( osteonecrosis ). tell your doctor and dentist immediately if you experience such symptoms while being treated with zoledronic acid teva or after stopping zyprexa . tell your doctor immediately if you develop any of these symptoms . other side effects very common side effects ( may affect more than 1 in 10 people ) low level of white blood cells , red blood cells and / or white blood cells ( which are important in fighting infection ) decreased appetite feeling sleepiness ( sleepiness ), sleepiness , sleepiness , tremor , unusual movements ( dyskinesias ) drowsiness , lack of energy ( fatigue ), lack of energy ( fatigue ), muscle cramps , lack of energy ( hypertonia ), tremor ( involuntary trembling ) sensation of heart beat ( tachycardia ) abnormal sensation of the lungs . uncommon side effects ( may affect up to 1 in 100 people ) serious allergic ( hypersensitivity ) reactions , including swollen face , tongue or throat which may be fatal and life - threatening allergic reactions . symptoms of swelling and pain , and / or pain in the joints , which may travel through blood vessels to the lungs causing bruising and pain in the upper left side of the body . this includes any possible side effects not listed in this leaflet .
